    <li> I bought this item through Amazon via one of the third party sellers. Amazon only sells it as an add-on item for $6.43 (at the time of this review) whereas the third party seller had it for $0.60 with free shipping. I admit that the extremely low price made me wonder what condition it would be in when/if it showed up, but I was happy to receive an unbroken set with no loose metal ends. As other reviewers have noted, you won&#x27;t actually get 10 different sizes since some of the ends are the same. I used a pair of digital calipers (accurate to +/- 0.02mm) to check the diameter of each end. The set I received had the following sizes (in mm):&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Green: 3.00/1.56&lt;br /&gt;Blue: 2.58/1.57&lt;br /&gt;White: 2.28/1.56&lt;br /&gt;Orange: 1.54/1.57&lt;br /&gt;Pink: 1.06/1.53&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I would say that there are really only 5 distinct sizes since the ends in the 1.53-1.57mm range are close enough that the difference is pretty much negligible and can probably be attributed to inconsistency in the measuring device or manufacturing process. While I would have liked to see 10 distinct sizes, the price was low enough that I&#x27;m satisfied with the purchase and would go ahead and recommend it to others as long as they know that half of the ends are basically the same.</li>

    <li> I&#x27;m pretty obsessed with all things manicure-related, and it wasn&#x27;t until recently that I started getting into my own nail art designs instead of those stick-on decals and stick-on polish kits. I figured that this kit would be a great start, and I believe that I made an excellent choice. For the price, you can&#x27;t beat it!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The dotting tools are perfect for simple designs, such as marbleizing or basic art, such as the &amp;#34;quilt&amp;#34; look, or even constellations. I&#x27;ve done quite a few different designs with these bad boys, and they&#x27;ve all turned out perfectly.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;What you should know before purchasing these dotting pens is that they are just that: Dotting tools.     <li> I ordered Dotting 5 X 2 Way Marbleizing Dotting Pen Set for Nail Art Manicure Pedicure, 4 Ounce. In the picture of the product I ordered, it showed all pink tools, which I didn&#x27;t care for. I placed this order on June 26th 2014, and it arrived on July 14, 2014. Given that it is shipped from Shen Zhen, China to Hawaii, this is pretty quick. (Roughly 2 and 1/2 weeks). I plan to use these tools for both polymer clay crafting, and nail art. Here is my Pros and Cons upon opening the package and first sight impression.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Here are the Cons:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;*False appearance advertising - colors: My first impression was the fact that I was expecting all pink tools. When I opened my package, I received tools that came in green, blue, white, pink, and orange. Although the color of the tools don&#x27;t bother me, this is just a generalization awareness that imagery posted on the product page is not accurate, so if you&#x27;re concerned about color, this is to let you know that imagery posted and product received is different, color-wise.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;*False appearance advertising - dotting size: If you look closely on the product image (one with all the pink tools) that was posted, both ends have different sizes that would escalate from small to big. This is not true. I lined up my tools from the dot size being small to big on one end, but when I looked at the other end, all the dot size were the same. I even measured it with a ruler, and they were all the same size that measures 1/16 inches. I ended up with 6 dot sizes being 1/16&amp;#34;, and the rest being different size. Just to forewarn ahead of time that you are not guaranteed 10 different dot size.  I guess this depends on the merchant as I have read from other reviews saying they received pens that came in 10 different size??&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;*Packaging - material: My package came in a very small bubble envelope mailer. I couldn&#x27;t rip the envelope open with my hands, so I decided to cut it open with a pair of scissors. I cut off the top of the envelope, and not knowingly, I&#x27;ve also cut off a small portion of the case that holds the tools. The case that holds the tools is a cheap quality plastic case. The best way to describe this material is probably a plastic beach bag, but more flimsy. A tip for those looking into keeping the plastic case: If you also need to cut open your package, cut from the side carefully, then pull the envelope apart. I do not plan to keep this case, so damaging the case upon opening the product did not bother me.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;For now, these are all the cons. I will update if there are more I find later, but these cons are general first contact with the product.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Here are the Pros:&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Great for crafting: As mentioned above, I plan to use these tools as a part of my crafting needs. Polymer Clay in particular, so for a cheap price of $2 this is not all that bad.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Sturdyness: I was worried about the tools falling apart as some other customer reviews had mentioned, but my tools were sturdy. The dot heads sit firmly on top of the pen shaped tool.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Size: The length of this pen fits nicely in my hands. (holding length is about 3 and 15/16&amp;#34;, total length from tip end to tip end measures 5 and 1/16&amp;#34;) I have very small hands and holding these tools don&#x27;t seem to be a problem for me.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Variety colors : As mentioned above, I expected my set to come in all pink, but the variation colors that was sent to me would help me recognize the dot size easily.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;All in all, there are pros and cons to these dotting pens. Surely, it is cheaper than to go out and buy expensive tools. If you&#x27;re looking for variation of dot sizes, it&#x27;s a gamble whether you&#x27;ll receive what you see in the images that were posted. Keep in mind that shipping speed varies, so if you&#x27;re in a hurry, this may not be the best option for you. If you&#x27;re looking into using these tools for your crafting needs, they make wonderful dimples, dots, and sometimes, better thanusing a paintbrush. Although the case is not the best case out there, I do not plan on keeping the case, because it has this rubbery nasty smell to it. I hope this review will help you determine your decision on purchasing this product.using a paintbrush. Although the case is not the best case out there, I do not plan on keeping the case, because it has this rubbery nasty smell to it. I hope this review will help you determine your decision on purchasing this product.</li>
